<div id="review_2010047145" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2010047145" />
    <a title="PorshaJo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5464046-porshajo"><img alt="PorshaJo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451425289p2/5464046.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2010047145?book_show_action=true">Feb 28, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="PorshaJo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="PorshaJo" href="/user/show/5464046-porshajo">PorshaJo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5464046-porshajo?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5464046-porshajo?shelf=challengereads-2018">challengereads-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5464046-porshajo?shelf=favorites-2018">favorites-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5464046-porshajo?shelf=challengereads">challengereads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2010047145" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5469610985168695537">Rating 4.75<br/><br/>Love! I just love this one! A special heart-warming book that should be read by everyone! It puts you through so many emotions while reading it. I laughed, I gasped, and I tried *really* hard not to cry. Note to self - don't read this book in public on the next read. The odd looks when you laugh out loud. I resisted for so long, worried about all the hype. But this is one time where you can believe that hype.<br/><br/>The Heart's Invisible Furries tells the life story of Cyril Avery, well, he's</span>
  <span id="freeText5469610985168695537" style="display:none">Rating 4.75<br /><br />Love! I just love this one! A special heart-warming book that should be read by everyone! It puts you through so many emotions while reading it. I laughed, I gasped, and I tried *really* hard not to cry. Note to self - don't read this book in public on the next read. The odd looks when you laugh out loud. I resisted for so long, worried about all the hype. But this is one time where you can believe that hype.<br /><br />The Heart's Invisible Furries tells the life story of Cyril Avery, well, he's not a REAL Avery. Told in various years from his birth to almost the end, told in 7 year spans. He was born to a very young, un-wed girl in Ireland in the early 1940's, which is blasphemy. She is cast out of her church, her home, her family, and her town by the local priest. After all, the priests in Ireland pretty much run everything and tell people how THEY should live. Eventually, Cyril is adopted by Charles (love him) and Maude Avery and spends his early childhood with them. Quite the odd "family" dynamic here but it leaves a lasting impression on Cyril. Cyril knows early on that he is a gay man, but it's a crime in Ireland. So begins his life. He goes through many trials and tribulations and heartache over the years. You watch as he leaves Ireland, moving to Amsterdam, New York, and eventually back to Ireland. Cyril is a bit of an odd one at times, sometimes so aloof, he appears clueless. Which made me love him even more. So many wonderful, unforgettable characters in this one. So many topics covered such as politics, bigotry, racism, love, death, violence, illness, marriage, and I can go on and on. But I don't want to give anything away.<br /><br />My only issue with this one is so many things in Cyril's life seemed to have way too many coincidences. So I had to knock it a bit for that. No one's life has that much fate intervening. But in the end, I loved it. And the audio....LOVED IT! Seriously, one of the best audios I've listened to in a very long time, and probably a favorite of mine. An actor can really do an audio justice and this was a perfect example. Stephen Hogan was fabulous. I highly suggest a listen to this audio. The book, it probably is in the top 10 of my all time favorites, and probably closer to the top. I'm looking for the print now and my only dilemma is.....do I read it, or listen to the audio the next time I revisit this one.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5469610985168695537" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

		<td>
		    <b>
          <a title="Diversity in All Forms!" class="actionLink" href="https://www.goodreads.com/topic/show/19830242-the-heart-s-invisible-furies-june-2019">Diversity in All ...:</a>
        </b>
      
			<a class="actionLink" href="/topic/show/19830242-the-heart-s-invisible-furies-june-2019"> The Heart&#39;s Invisible Furies (June 2019)</a>
		</td>
		<td class="nobreak">
		  15

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('pujRr+vtyAiVh9ULlVazBtUlemUsl5r4XAi+4s9+UWk3DMRUe0cnplyFII0OcmYqK1+r8Mq1IFvEUtndGvkCTA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('kNDBqAN07LPE2wD5qCpKARSZAjykE0oxPPI/EZo42jgBNNRTk94DHQ3Z9X8zDp8t6uPTqUIx8JKkqFguT7+JHQ==')})
  }

The cell phone service may be spotty and the waves may be rough, but every detail has been expertly planned and will be expertly executed.\n\nBut perfection is for plans, and people are all too human. <div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer16964555791845060432">John Boyne (born 30 April 1971 in Dublin) is an Irish novelist.<br/><br/>He was educated at Trinity College, Dublin, and studied Creative Writing at the University of East Anglia, where he won the Curtis Brown prize. In 2015, he was awarded an Honorary Doctorate of Letters by UEA.<br/><br/>John Boyne is the author of ten novels for adults and five for young readers, as well as a collection of short stories. <br/><br/>His novel</span>
  <span id="freeText16964555791845060432" style="display:none">John Boyne (born 30 April 1971 in Dublin) is an Irish novelist.<br /><br />He was educated at Trinity College, Dublin, and studied Creative Writing at the University of East Anglia, where he won the Curtis Brown prize. In 2015, he was awarded an Honorary Doctorate of Letters by UEA.<br /><br />John Boyne is the author of ten novels for adults and five for young readers, as well as a collection of short stories. <br /><br />His novels are published in over 50 languages. <br /><br /><i>The Boy in the Striped Pyjamas</i>, which to date has sold more than 7 million copies worldwide, is a #1 New York Times Bestseller and a film adaptation was released in September 2008. Boyne resides in Dublin. He is represented by the literary agent Simon Trewin at WME in London, United Kingdom.<br /><br />His most recent publication is the novel 'The Heart's Invisible Furies', published in the UK in February 2017. It will be published in the USA in August.<br /></span>
